# Core & Body Control Exercise Cards 1-50

Complete batch for Cursor/import work. Core & Body Control is treated as a quality-first methodology primarily belonging to Resilience and Movement Intelligence, with low-fatigue Prepare & Access activation/breathing exceptions.

          "Begin Crab Reach from the coached start position.",
          "Move slowly enough that the trunk, pelvis, shoulder, and hip positions remain organized.",
          "Breathe behind the brace instead of holding air or grinding.",
          "Pause briefly at the hardest point, then return under control.",
          "Stop the set when the athlete cannot repeat the same position."
        ],
        "coach_cues": [
          "Ribs over pelvis.",
          "Breathe behind the brace.",
          "Move only through the range you own.",
          "Quiet hips, quiet ribs.",
          "Stop before the position changes."
        ],
